Draining occurs\n621:   // either when a connection hits the idle timeout, when :ref:`max_connection_duration\n622:   // <envoy_v3_api_field_config.core.v3.HttpProtocolOptions.max_connection_duration>`\n623:   // is reached, or during general server draining.
